\"text\": \"## Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration Guide\\n\\nIn Apache Kafka's Streams library, the DSL (Domain Specific Language) operations are implemented as thin wrappers around the lower-level Processor API. This enables teams to migrate from the high-level DSL to the Processor API for fine-grained control over state store management.\\n\\n### Key Architectural Pattern\\n\\nEach DSL operation in the `org.apache.kafka.streams.kstream.internals` package implements either `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` or `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` from the `org.apache.kafka.streams.processor.api` package. These supplier implementations return concrete Processor instances that extend either `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`.\\n\\n### Stream Operations (KStream DSL)\\n\\n#### Transformation Operations\\n\\n1. **KStreamMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Maps both key and value transformations using `KeyValueMapper`.\\n\\n2. **KStreamFilter.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner `KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Filters records using a `Predicate`, supporting both filter and filterNot operations.\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Transforms only the value while keeping the key unchanged.\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Produces multiple output records per input record, transforming both key and value.\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Produces multiple values per input record while preserving the key.\\n\\n6. **KStreamBranch.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with inner `KStreamBranchProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Routes records to different child nodes based on predicates.\\n\\n7. **KStreamPeek.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Performs side-effect operations without modifying records.\\n\\n8. **KStreamPrint.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, Void, Void>` for printing records to output.\\n\\n#### Aggregation Operations\\n\\n9. **KStreamAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Uses state stores for stateful aggregation with custom initializer and aggregator functions.\\n\\n10. **KStreamReduce.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KStreamReduceProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Reduces stream records using a reducer function, maintaining state in a store.\\n\\n11. **KStreamWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Performs time-windowed aggregation with configurable window semantics.\\n\\n12. **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Implements session-windowed aggregation for event-time based windowing.\\n\\n13. **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Provides sliding window semantics for aggregations.\\n\\n#### Join Operations\\n\\n14. **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K1, V1, K1, VOut>`. Joins a stream with a global table using a `KeyValueMapper` to extract the join key.\\n\\n15. **KStreamKStreamJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, VThis, K, VOut>` with inner `KStreamKStreamJoinProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Joins two streams with windowed join semantics.\\n\\n16. **KStreamKStreamSelfJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V1, K, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Joins a stream with itself using window store.\\n\\n17. **KStreamKTableJoinProcessor.java** - Extends `ContextualProcessor` directly. Used by stream-table join operations to look up table values.\\n\\n### Table Operations (KTable DSL)\\n\\n18. **KTableMapValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>` with `KTableMapValuesProcessor`. Transforms table values while preserving keys, supporting both materialized and non-materialized views.\\n\\n19. **KTableFilter.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>` with `KTableFilterProcessor`. Filters table records while maintaining state.\\n\\n20. **KTableAggregate.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KTableAggregateProcessor`. Aggregates table values using initializer and aggregator functions with materialized state stores.\\n\\n21. **KTableReduce.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KTableReduceProcessor`. Reduces table records using add and remove reducers for both forward and reverse aggregations.\\n\\n22. **KTableTransformValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, VOut>` with `KTableTransformValuesProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Applies custom value transformation logic using `ValueTransformerWithKey`.\\n\\n### Main Implementation Classes\\n\\n23. **KStreamImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KStream` interface. Provides public API methods like `map()`, `filter()`, `flatMap()`, and delegates to corresponding internal processor suppliers.\\n\\n24. **KGroupedStreamImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedStream` interface for operations that follow `groupByKey()` or `groupBy()`, including aggregate, reduce, and windowing operations.\\n\\n25. **KTableImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KTable` interface. Provides methods like `mapValues()`, `filter()`, and aggregate operations.\\n\\n26. **KGroupedTableImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedTable` interface for aggregation and reduction operations on grouped tables.\\n\\n### Migration Path\\n\\nTo migrate from DSL to the Processor API for custom state store management:\\n\\n1. Replace DSL operations (e.g., `stream.map(...)`) with equivalent `Processor` implementations\\n2. Create custom `ProcessorSupplier` classes that provide your `Processor` instances\\n3. Use `topology.addProcessor()` instead of DSL methods to add processors to the topology\\n4. Manually create and attach state stores using `topology.addStateStore()`\\n5. Reference custom state stores in your processor using `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\nThe Processor API provides:\\n- Direct access to `ProcessorContext` for state store management\\n- Fine-grained control over record forwarding and scheduling punctuation\\n- Custom state store selection and lifecycle management\\n- Lower-level performance optimizations when needed\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1586,"cache_read_input_tokens":83226,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1586},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"31c4cb8d-c9c0-4a7e-a240-1fab84fa40e6","uuid":"67abc810-e69b-44b4-b0a9-7765ed2cc1d1"}

\"text\": \"## Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration Guide\\n\\nIn Apache Kafka's Streams library, the DSL (Domain Specific Language) operations are implemented as thin wrappers around the lower-level Processor API. This enables teams to migrate from the high-level DSL to the Processor API for fine-grained control over state store management.\\n\\n### Key Architectural Pattern\\n\\nEach DSL operation in the `org.apache.kafka.streams.kstream.internals` package implements either `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` or `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` from the `org.apache.kafka.streams.processor.api` package. These supplier implementations return concrete Processor instances that extend either `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`.\\n\\n### Stream Operations (KStream DSL)\\n\\n#### Transformation Operations\\n\\n1. **KStreamMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Maps both key and value transformations using `KeyValueMapper`.\\n\\n2. **KStreamFilter.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner `KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Filters records using a `Predicate`, supporting both filter and filterNot operations.\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Transforms only the value while keeping the key unchanged.\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Produces multiple output records per input record, transforming both key and value.\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Produces multiple values per input record while preserving the key.\\n\\n6. **KStreamBranch.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with inner `KStreamBranchProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Routes records to different child nodes based on predicates.\\n\\n7. **KStreamPeek.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Performs side-effect operations without modifying records.\\n\\n8. **KStreamPrint.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, Void, Void>` for printing records to output.\\n\\n#### Aggregation Operations\\n\\n9. **KStreamAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Uses state stores for stateful aggregation with custom initializer and aggregator functions.\\n\\n10. **KStreamReduce.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KStreamReduceProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Reduces stream records using a reducer function, maintaining state in a store.\\n\\n11. **KStreamWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Performs time-windowed aggregation with configurable window semantics.\\n\\n12. **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Implements session-windowed aggregation for event-time based windowing.\\n\\n13. **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Provides sliding window semantics for aggregations.\\n\\n#### Join Operations\\n\\n14. **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K1, V1, K1, VOut>`. Joins a stream with a global table using a `KeyValueMapper` to extract the join key.\\n\\n15. **KStreamKStreamJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, VThis, K, VOut>` with inner `KStreamKStreamJoinProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Joins two streams with windowed join semantics.\\n\\n16. **KStreamKStreamSelfJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V1, K, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Joins a stream with itself using window store.\\n\\n17. **KStreamKTableJoinProcessor.java** - Extends `ContextualProcessor` directly. Used by stream-table join operations to look up table values.\\n\\n### Table Operations (KTable DSL)\\n\\n18. **KTableMapValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>` with `KTableMapValuesProcessor`. Transforms table values while preserving keys, supporting both materialized and non-materialized views.\\n\\n19. **KTableFilter.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>` with `KTableFilterProcessor`. Filters table records while maintaining state.\\n\\n20. **KTableAggregate.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KTableAggregateProcessor`. Aggregates table values using initializer and aggregator functions with materialized state stores.\\n\\n21. **KTableReduce.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KTableReduceProcessor`. Reduces table records using add and remove reducers for both forward and reverse aggregations.\\n\\n22. **KTableTransformValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, VOut>` with `KTableTransformValuesProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Applies custom value transformation logic using `ValueTransformerWithKey`.\\n\\n### Main Implementation Classes\\n\\n23. **KStreamImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KStream` interface. Provides public API methods like `map()`, `filter()`, `flatMap()`, and delegates to corresponding internal processor suppliers.\\n\\n24. **KGroupedStreamImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedStream` interface for operations that follow `groupByKey()` or `groupBy()`, including aggregate, reduce, and windowing operations.\\n\\n25. **KTableImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KTable` interface. Provides methods like `mapValues()`, `filter()`, and aggregate operations.\\n\\n26. **KGroupedTableImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedTable` interface for aggregation and reduction operations on grouped tables.\\n\\n### Migration Path\\n\\nTo migrate from DSL to the Processor API for custom state store management:\\n\\n1. Replace DSL operations (e.g., `stream.map(...)`) with equivalent `Processor` implementations\\n2. Create custom `ProcessorSupplier` classes that provide your `Processor` instances\\n3. Use `topology.addProcessor()` instead of DSL methods to add processors to the topology\\n4. Manually create and attach state stores using `topology.addStateStore()`\\n5. Reference custom state stores in your processor using `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\nThe Processor API provides:\\n- Direct access to `ProcessorContext` for state store management\\n- Fine-grained control over record forwarding and scheduling punctuation\\n- Custom state store selection and lifecycle management\\n- Lower-level performance optimizations when needed\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

  }\n   219→  ],\n   220→  \"text\": \"## Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration Guide\\n\\nIn Apache Kafka's Streams library, the DSL (Domain Specific Language) operations are implemented as thin wrappers around the lower-level Processor API. This enables teams to migrate from the high-level DSL to the Processor API for fine-grained control over state store management.\\n\\n### Key Architectural Pattern\\n\\nEach DSL operation in the `org.apache.kafka.streams.kstream.internals` package implements either `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` or `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` from the `org.apache.kafka.streams.processor.api` package. These supplier implementations return concrete Processor instances that extend either `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`.\\n\\n### Stream Operations (KStream DSL)\\n\\n#### Transformation Operations\\n\\n1. **KStreamMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Maps both key and value transformations using `KeyValueMapper`.\\n\\n2. **KStreamFilter.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner `KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Filters records using a `Predicate`, supporting both filter and filterNot operations.\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Transforms only the value while keeping the key unchanged.\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Produces multiple output records per input record, transforming both key and value.\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Produces multiple values per input record while preserving the key.\\n\\n6. **KStreamBranch.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with inner `KStreamBranchProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Routes records to different child nodes based on predicates.\\n\\n7. **KStreamPeek.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Performs side-effect operations without modifying records.\\n\\n8. **KStreamPrint.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, Void, Void>` for printing records to output.\\n\\n#### Aggregation Operations\\n\\n9. **KStreamAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Uses state stores for stateful aggregation with custom initializer and aggregator functions.\\n\\n10. **KStreamReduce.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KStreamReduceProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Reduces stream records using a reducer function, maintaining state in a store.\\n\\n11. **KStreamWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Performs time-windowed aggregation with configurable window semantics.\\n\\n12. **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Implements session-windowed aggregation for event-time based windowing.\\n\\n13. **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Provides sliding window semantics for aggregations.\\n\\n#### Join Operations\\n\\n14. **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K1, V1, K1, VOut>`. Joins a stream with a global table using a `KeyValueMapper` to extract the join key.\\n\\n15. **KStreamKStreamJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, VThis, K, VOut>` with inner `KStreamKStreamJoinProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Joins two streams with windowed join semantics.\\n\\n16. **KStreamKStreamSelfJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V1, K, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Joins a stream with itself using window store.\\n\\n17. **KStreamKTableJoinProcessor.java** - Extends `ContextualProcessor` directly. Used by stream-table join operations to look up table values.\\n\\n### Table Operations (KTable DSL)\\n\\n18. **KTableMapValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>` with `KTableMapValuesProcessor`. Transforms table values while preserving keys, supporting both materialized and non-materialized views.\\n\\n19. **KTableFilter.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>` with `KTableFilterProcessor`. Filters table records while maintaining state.\\n\\n20. **KTableAggregate.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KTableAggregateProcessor`. Aggregates table values using initializer and aggregator functions with materialized state stores.\\n\\n21. **KTableReduce.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KTableReduceProcessor`. Reduces table records using add and remove reducers for both forward and reverse aggregations.\\n\\n22. **KTableTransformValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, VOut>` with `KTableTransformValuesProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Applies custom value transformation logic using `ValueTransformerWithKey`.\\n\\n### Main Implementation Classes\\n\\n23. **KStreamImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KStream` interface. Provides public API methods like `map()`, `filter()`, `flatMap()`, and delegates to corresponding internal processor suppliers.\\n\\n24. **KGroupedStreamImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedStream` interface for operations that follow `groupByKey()` or `groupBy()`, including aggregate, reduce, and windowing operations.\\n\\n25. **KTableImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KTable` interface. Provides methods like `mapValues()`, `filter()`, and aggregate operations.\\n\\n26. **KGroupedTableImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedTable` interface for aggregation and reduction operations on grouped tables.\\n\\n### Migration Path\\n\\nTo migrate from DSL to the Processor API for custom state store management:\\n\\n1. Replace DSL operations (e.g., `stream.map(...)`) with equivalent `Processor` implementations\\n2. Create custom `ProcessorSupplier` classes that provide your `Processor` instances\\n3. Use `topology.addProcessor()` instead of DSL methods to add processors to the topology\\n4. Manually create and attach state stores using `topology.addStateStore()`\\n5. Reference custom state stores in your processor using `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\nThe Processor API provides:\\n- Direct access to `ProcessorContext` for state store management\\n- Fine-grained control over record forwarding and scheduling punctuation\\n- Custom state store selection and lifecycle management\\n- Lower-level performance optimizations when needed\"\n   221→}\n   222→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. \"text\": \"## Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration Guide\\n\\nIn Apache Kafka's Streams library, the DSL (Domain Specific Language) operations are implemented as thin wrappers around the lower-level Processor API. This enables teams to migrate from the high-level DSL to the Processor API for fine-grained control over state store management.\\n\\n### Key Architectural Pattern\\n\\nEach DSL operation in the `org.apache.kafka.streams.kstream.internals` package implements either `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` or `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` from the `org.apache.kafka.streams.processor.api` package. These supplier implementations return concrete Processor instances that extend either `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`.\\n\\n### Stream Operations (KStream DSL)\\n\\n#### Transformation Operations\\n\\n1. **KStreamMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Maps both key and value transformations using `KeyValueMapper`.\\n\\n2. **KStreamFilter.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner `KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Filters records using a `Predicate`, supporting both filter and filterNot operations.\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Transforms only the value while keeping the key unchanged.\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Produces multiple output records per input record, transforming both key and value.\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Produces multiple values per input record while preserving the key.\\n\\n6. **KStreamBranch.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with inner `KStreamBranchProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Routes records to different child nodes based on predicates.\\n\\n7. **KStreamPeek.java** - Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>` with inner processor extending `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`. Performs side-effect operations without modifying records.\\n\\n8. **KStreamPrint.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, Void, Void>` for printing records to output.\\n\\n#### Aggregation Operations\\n\\n9. **KStreamAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Uses state stores for stateful aggregation with custom initializer and aggregator functions.\\n\\n10. **KStreamReduce.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KStreamReduceProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Reduces stream records using a reducer function, maintaining state in a store.\\n\\n11. **KStreamWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Performs time-windowed aggregation with configurable window semantics.\\n\\n12. **KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Implements session-windowed aggregation for event-time based windowing.\\n\\n13. **KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java** - Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, Windowed<KIn>, VAgg>`. Provides sliding window semantics for aggregations.\\n\\n#### Join Operations\\n\\n14. **KStreamGlobalKTableJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K1, V1, K1, VOut>`. Joins a stream with a global table using a `KeyValueMapper` to extract the join key.\\n\\n15. **KStreamKStreamJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, VThis, K, VOut>` with inner `KStreamKStreamJoinProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Joins two streams with windowed join semantics.\\n\\n16. **KStreamKStreamSelfJoin.java** - Implements `ProcessorSupplier<K, V1, K, VOut>` with inner processor extending `ContextualProcessor`. Joins a stream with itself using window store.\\n\\n17. **KStreamKTableJoinProcessor.java** - Extends `ContextualProcessor` directly. Used by stream-table join operations to look up table values.\\n\\n### Table Operations (KTable DSL)\\n\\n18. **KTableMapValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>` with `KTableMapValuesProcessor`. Transforms table values while preserving keys, supporting both materialized and non-materialized views.\\n\\n19. **KTableFilter.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>` with `KTableFilterProcessor`. Filters table records while maintaining state.\\n\\n20. **KTableAggregate.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>` with `KTableAggregateProcessor`. Aggregates table values using initializer and aggregator functions with materialized state stores.\\n\\n21. **KTableReduce.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, V>` with `KTableReduceProcessor`. Reduces table records using add and remove reducers for both forward and reverse aggregations.\\n\\n22. **KTableTransformValues.java** - Implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<K, V, K, VOut>` with `KTableTransformValuesProcessor extends ContextualProcessor`. Applies custom value transformation logic using `ValueTransformerWithKey`.\\n\\n### Main Implementation Classes\\n\\n23. **KStreamImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KStream` interface. Provides public API methods like `map()`, `filter()`, `flatMap()`, and delegates to corresponding internal processor suppliers.\\n\\n24. **KGroupedStreamImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedStream` interface for operations that follow `groupByKey()` or `groupBy()`, including aggregate, reduce, and windowing operations.\\n\\n25. **KTableImpl.java** - Core implementation of the `KTable` interface. Provides methods like `mapValues()`, `filter()`, and aggregate operations.\\n\\n26. **KGroupedTableImpl.java** - Implements the `KGroupedTable` interface for aggregation and reduction operations on grouped tables.\\n\\n### Migration Path\\n\\nTo migrate from DSL to the Processor API for custom state store management:\\n\\n1. Replace DSL operations (e.g., `stream.map(...)`) with equivalent `Processor` implementations\\n2. Create custom `ProcessorSupplier` classes that provide your `Processor` instances\\n3. Use `topology.addProcessor()` instead of DSL methods to add processors to the topology\\n4. Manually create and attach state stores using `topology.addStateStore()`\\n5. Reference custom state stores in your processor using `context().getStateStore(storeName)`\\n\\nThe Processor API provides:\\n- Direct access to `ProcessorContext` for state store management\\n- Fine-grained control over record forwarding and scheduling punctuation\\n- Custom state store selection and lifecycle management\\n- Lower-level performance optimizations when needed\"\n}\n","numLines":222,"startLine":1,"totalLines":222}}}
